  Defined.

  Definition coproduct_of_limit_to_limit_of_coproduct
    : coproduct_of_limit --> lim limit_of_coproduct
    := pr11 (isLimCone_LimCone limit_of_coproduct _ limit_of_coproduct_as_cone_of_coproduct_to_limit).

  Definition coproduct_distribute_over_omega_limits : UU
    := is_z_isomorphism coproduct_of_limit_to_limit_of_coproduct.

End OmegaLimitsCommutingWithCoproducts.

Definition ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts
           (C : category) (I : HSET)
           (ω_lim : Lims_of_shape conat_graph C)
           (coprd : Coproducts (pr1 I) C)
  : UU := ∏ ind, coproduct_distribute_over_omega_limits C ω_lim coprd ind.

(*
A coproducts of omega-continuous functors is in general not omega-continuous.
This boils down to the commutativity of ω-limits and coproducts.
*)
Section CoproductOfFunctorsContinuity.

  Context (D : category) (I : HSET) (ω_lim : Lims_of_shape conat_graph D) (CP : Coproducts (pr1 I) D).

  
D: category
I: SET
ω_lim: Lims_of_shape conat_graph D
CP: Coproducts (pr1 I) D
C: category
Lims_of_shape conat_graph [C, D]

  
D: category
I: SET
ω_lim: Lims_of_shape conat_graph D
CP: Coproducts (pr1 I) D
C: category
Lims_of_shape conat_graph [C, D]

    apply LimsFunctorCategory_of_shape, ω_lim.
  Defined.

  Let coproduct_functor_cat (C : category) : Coproducts (pr1 I) [C,D]
    := Coproducts_functor_precat (pr1 I) C D CP.

  
D: category
I: SET
ω_lim: Lims_of_shape conat_graph D
CP: Coproducts (pr1 I) D
coproduct_functor_cat:= λ C : category,
Coproducts_functor_precat
  (pr1 I) C D CP: ∏ C : category,
Coproducts (pr1 I) [C, D]
ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts D I ω_lim CP
→ ∏ C : category,
  ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts [C, D] I
    (ω_complete_functor_cat C)
    (coproduct_functor_cat C)

  
D: category
I: SET
ω_lim: Lims_of_shape conat_graph D
CP: Coproducts (pr1 I) D
coproduct_functor_cat:= λ C : category,
Coproducts_functor_precat
  (pr1 I) C D CP: ∏ C : category,
Coproducts (pr1 I) [C, D]
ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts D I ω_lim CP
→ ∏ C : category,
  ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts [C, D] I
    (ω_complete_functor_cat C)
    (coproduct_functor_cat C)

    
D: category
I: SET
ω_lim: Lims_of_shape conat_graph D
CP: Coproducts (pr1 I) D
coproduct_functor_cat:= λ C : category,
Coproducts_functor_precat
  (pr1 I) C D CP: ∏ C : category,
Coproducts (pr1 I) [C, D]
distr: ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts D I
  ω_lim CP
C: category

Coproducts_functor_precat
  (pr1 I) C D CP: ∏ C : category,
Coproducts (pr1 I) [C, D]
distr: ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts D I
  ω_lim CP
C: category
ind: pr1 I → cochain [C, D]
c: C
ind_c:= λ i : pr1 I,
(λ n : vertex conat_graph,
 pr1 (dob (ind i) n) c),,
(λ (n m : vertex conat_graph) 
 (p : edge n m), pr1 (dmor (ind i) p) c): pr1 I → cochain D
u: vertex conat_graph
pr1
  (coproduct_of_limit_to_limit_of_coproduct [C, D]
     (ω_complete_functor_cat C)
     (coproduct_functor_cat C) ind) c
· limOut
    (ω_lim
       (diagram_pointwise
          (coproduct_n_cochain [C, D]
             (coproduct_functor_cat C) ind) c)) u =
coneOut
  (limit_of_coproduct_as_cone_of_coproduct_to_limit D
     ω_lim CP ind_c) u

       (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i))))

CP: Coproducts (pr1 I) D
coproduct_functor_cat:= λ C : category,
Coproducts_functor_precat
  (pr1 I) C D CP: ∏ C : category,
Coproducts (pr1 I) [C, D]
C: category
F: pr1 I → C ⟶ D
ω_distr: ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts D I
  ω_lim CP
Fi_cont: ∏ i : pr1 I, is_omega_cont (F i)
coch: cochain C
l: C
l_cone: cone coch l
l_lim: isLimCone coch l l_cone
ind:= λ i : pr1 I,
(λ n : vertex conat_graph, F i (dob coch n)),,
(λ (n m : vertex conat_graph) 
 (p : edge n m), # (F i) (dmor coch p)): pr1 I → cochain D
distr:= ω_distr ind: coproduct_distribute_over_omega_limits D ω_lim
  CP ind
distr1:= pr1 distr: D
⟦ lim (ω_lim (coproduct_n_cochain D CP ind)),
CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i))) ⟧
i_iso:= CoproductOfArrowsIsos (pr1 I) D
  (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i)))
  (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i))))
  (λ i : pr1 I, F i l)
  (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l))
  (λ i : pr1 I,
   limArrow
     (make_LimCone (mapdiagram (F i) coch)
        (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
        (Fi_cont i coch l l_cone l_lim))
     (lim (ω_lim (ind i)))
     (limCone (ω_lim (ind i))))
  (λ i : pr1 I,
   let Fi_l := Fi_cont i coch l l_cone l_lim in
   pr2
     (z_iso_inv
        (limArrow (ω_lim (ind i)) 
           (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone),,
         isLim_is_z_iso 
           (mapdiagram (F i) coch)
           (ω_lim (ind i)) 
           (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
           Fi_l))): is_z_isomorphism
  (CoproductOfArrows (pr1 I) D
     (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i))))
     (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l))
     (λ i : pr1 I,
      limArrow
        (make_LimCone (mapdiagram (F i) coch)
           (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
           (Fi_cont i coch l l_cone l_lim))
        (lim (ω_lim (ind i)))
        (limCone (ω_lim (ind i)))))
i: pr1 I
?b =
limArrow (ω_lim (ind i)) 
  (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
· CoproductIn (pr1 I) D
    (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i)))) i

  (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i)))

   limArrow
     (make_LimCone (mapdiagram (F i) coch)

           (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
           Fi_l))): is_z_isomorphism

     (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i))))
     (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l))

        (limCone (ω_lim (ind i)))))

· limArrow
    (ω_lim
       (mapdiagram
          (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F)
          coch))
    (coproduct_of_functors_ob (pr1 I) C D CP F l)
    (mapcone (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F)
       coch l_cone) · distr1 =
limArrow (ω_lim (ind i)) (F i l)
  (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)

    (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i)))) i

l_cone: cone coch l

  (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i)))

  (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l))
  (λ i : pr1 I,
   limArrow
     (make_LimCone (mapdiagram (F i) coch)
        (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
        (Fi_cont i coch l l_cone l_lim))

     (z_iso_inv

           Fi_l))): is_z_isomorphism
  (CoproductOfArrows (pr1 I) D
     (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i))))
     (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l))
     (λ i : pr1 I,
      limArrow
        (make_LimCone (mapdiagram (F i) coch)
           (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
           (Fi_cont i coch l l_cone l_lim))
        (lim (ω_lim (ind i)))
        (limCone (ω_lim (ind i)))))
i: pr1 I
limArrow
  (ω_lim
     (mapdiagram
        (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F) coch))
  (F i l)
  (make_cone
     (λ u : vertex conat_graph,
      CoproductIn (pr1 I) D (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l))
        i
      · coneOut
          (mapcone
             (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F)
             coch l_cone) u)
     (Cone_precompose
        (mapcone
           (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F)
           coch l_cone) (F i l)
        (CoproductIn (pr1 I) D
           (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l)) i))) · distr1 =
limArrow (ω_lim (ind i)) (F i l)
  (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
· CoproductIn (pr1 I) D
    (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i)))) i

     (mapdiagram
        (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F) coch))

        (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l)) i
      · coneOut
          (mapcone
             (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F)

        (mapcone
           (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F)

        (F i l)

           (CP (λ i : pr1 I, F i l)) i))) =

  (F i l) (mapcone (F i) coch l_cone)
· CoproductIn (pr1 I) D
    (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i)))) i
· inv_from_z_iso (distr1,, ?pr2)

ω_distr: ω_limits_distribute_over_I_coproducts D I
  ω_lim CP
Fi_cont: ∏ i : pr1 I, is_omega_cont (F i)
coch: cochain C
l: C
l_cone: cone coch l
l_lim: isLimCone coch l l_cone
ind:= λ i : pr1 I,
(λ n : vertex conat_graph, F i (dob coch n)),,
(λ (n m : vertex conat_graph) 
 (p : edge n m), # (F i) (dmor coch p)): pr1 I → cochain D
distr:= ω_distr ind: coproduct_distribute_over_omega_limits D ω_lim
  CP ind
distr1:= pr1 distr: D
⟦ lim (ω_lim (coproduct_n_cochain D CP ind)),
CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i))) ⟧
inv_from_z_iso
  (pr1 distr,,
   pr2
     (z_iso_inv
        (coproduct_of_limit_to_limit_of_coproduct D
           ω_lim CP ind,, distr)))
· identity
    (lim
       (ω_lim
          (mapdiagram
             (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F)
             coch))) = ?b

  (CP (λ i : pr1 I, lim (ω_lim (ind i))))

          (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F)
          coch)) n = ?t2

          apply (limArrowCommutes  (ω_lim (mapdiagram (coproduct_of_functors (pr1 I) C D CP F) coch))).
